   66 import Data.Char (ord)

   69 -- | Encode a Haskell String to a list of Word8 values, in UTF8 format.
   70 utf8Encode :: Char -> [Word8]
   71 utf8Encode = uncurry (:) . utf8Encode'
   72 
   73 utf8Encode' :: Char -> (Word8, [Word8])
   74 utf8Encode' c = case go (ord c) of
   75                   (x, xs) -> (fromIntegral x, map fromIntegral xs)
   76  where
   77   go oc
   78    | oc <= 0x7f       = ( oc
   79                         , [
   80                         ])
   81 
   82    | oc <= 0x7ff      = ( 0xc0 + (oc `Data.Bits.shiftR` 6)
   83                         , [0x80 + oc Data.Bits..&. 0x3f
   84                         ])
   85 
   86    | oc <= 0xffff     = ( 0xe0 + (oc `Data.Bits.shiftR` 12)
   87                         , [0x80 + ((oc `Data.Bits.shiftR` 6) Data.Bits..&. 0x3f)
   88                         , 0x80 + oc Data.Bits..&. 0x3f
   89                         ])
   90    | otherwise        = ( 0xf0 + (oc `Data.Bits.shiftR` 18)
   91                         , [0x80 + ((oc `Data.Bits.shiftR` 12) Data.Bits..&. 0x3f)
   92                         , 0x80 + ((oc `Data.Bits.shiftR` 6) Data.Bits..&. 0x3f)
   93                         , 0x80 + oc Data.Bits..&. 0x3f
   94                         ])
   95 
   96 #endif
   97 
   98 type Byte = Word8
   99 
  100 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  101 -- The input type
  102 
  103 #if defined(ALEX_POSN) || defined(ALEX_MONAD) || defined(ALEX_GSCAN)
  104 type AlexInput = (AlexPosn,     -- current position,
  105                   Char,         -- previous char
  106                   [Byte],       -- pending bytes on current char
  107                   String)       -- current input string
  108 
  109 ignorePendingBytes :: AlexInput -> AlexInput
  110 ignorePendingBytes (p,c,_ps,s) = (p,c,[],s)
  111 
  112 alexInputPrevChar :: AlexInput -> Char
  113 alexInputPrevChar (_p,c,_bs,_s) = c
  114 
  115 alexGetByte :: AlexInput -> Maybe (Byte,AlexInput)
  116 alexGetByte (p,c,(b:bs),s) = Just (b,(p,c,bs,s))
  117 alexGetByte (_,_,[],[]) = Nothing
  118 alexGetByte (p,_,[],(c:s))  = let p' = alexMove p c
  119                               in case utf8Encode' c of
  120                                    (b, bs) -> p' `seq`  Just (b, (p', c, bs, s))
  121 #endif
  122 
  123 #if defined (ALEX_STRICT_TEXT)
  124 type AlexInput = (Char,           -- previous char
  125                   [Byte],         -- pending bytes on current char
  126                   Data.Text.Text) -- current input string
  127 
  128 ignorePendingBytes :: AlexInput -> AlexInput
  129 ignorePendingBytes (c,_ps,s) = (c,[],s)
  130 
  131 alexInputPrevChar :: AlexInput -> Char
  132 alexInputPrevChar (c,_bs,_s) = c
  133 
  134 alexGetByte :: AlexInput -> Maybe (Byte,AlexInput)
  135 alexGetByte (c,(b:bs),s) = Just (b,(c,bs,s))
  136 alexGetByte (_,[],s) = case Data.Text.uncons s of
  137                             Just (c, cs) ->
  138                               case utf8Encode' c of
  139                                 (b, bs) -> Just (b, (c, bs, cs))
  140                             Nothing ->
  141                               Nothing
  142 #endif
  143 
  144 #if defined (ALEX_POSN_STRICT_TEXT) || defined(ALEX_MONAD_STRICT_TEXT)
  145 type AlexInput = (AlexPosn,       -- current position,
  146                   Char,           -- previous char
  147                   [Byte],         -- pending bytes on current char
  148                   Data.Text.Text) -- current input string
  149 
  150 ignorePendingBytes :: AlexInput -> AlexInput
  151 ignorePendingBytes (p,c,_ps,s) = (p,c,[],s)
  152 
  153 alexInputPrevChar :: AlexInput -> Char
  154 alexInputPrevChar (_p,c,_bs,_s) = c
  155 
  156 alexGetByte :: AlexInput -> Maybe (Byte,AlexInput)
  157 alexGetByte (p,c,(b:bs),s) = Just (b,(p,c,bs,s))
  158 alexGetByte (p,_,[],s) = case Data.Text.uncons s of
  159                             Just (c, cs) ->
  160                               let p' = alexMove p c
  161                               in case utf8Encode' c of
  162                                    (b, bs) -> p' `seq`  Just (b, (p', c, bs, cs))
  163                             Nothing ->
  164                               Nothing
  165 #endif
  166 
  167 #if defined(ALEX_POSN_BYTESTRING) || defined(ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING)
  168 type AlexInput = (AlexPosn,     -- current position,
  169                   Char,         -- previous char
  170                   ByteString.ByteString,        -- current input string
  171                   Int64)           -- bytes consumed so far
  172 
  173 ignorePendingBytes :: AlexInput -> AlexInput
  174 ignorePendingBytes i = i   -- no pending bytes when lexing bytestrings
  175 
  176 alexInputPrevChar :: AlexInput -> Char
  177 alexInputPrevChar (_,c,_,_) = c
  178 
  179 alexGetByte :: AlexInput -> Maybe (Byte,AlexInput)
  180 alexGetByte (p,_,cs,n) =
  181     case ByteString.uncons cs of
  182         Nothing -> Nothing
  183         Just (b, cs') ->
  184             let c   = ByteString.w2c b
  185                 p'  = alexMove p c
  186                 n'  = n+1
  187             in p' `seq` cs' `seq` n' `seq` Just (b, (p', c, cs',n'))
  188 #endif
  189 
  190 #ifdef ALEX_BASIC_BYTESTRING
  191 data AlexInput = AlexInput { alexChar :: {-# UNPACK #-} !Char,      -- previous char
  192                              alexStr ::  !ByteString.ByteString,    -- current input string
  193                              alexBytePos :: {-# UNPACK #-} !Int64}  -- bytes consumed so far
  194 
  195 alexInputPrevChar :: AlexInput -> Char
  196 alexInputPrevChar = alexChar
  197 
  198 alexGetByte (AlexInput {alexStr=cs,alexBytePos=n}) =
  199     case ByteString.uncons cs of
  200         Nothing -> Nothing
  201         Just (c, rest) ->
  202             Just (c, AlexInput {
  203                 alexChar = ByteString.w2c c,
  204                 alexStr =  rest,
  205                 alexBytePos = n+1})
  206 #endif
  207 
  208 #ifdef ALEX_STRICT_BYTESTRING
  209 data AlexInput = AlexInput { alexChar :: {-# UNPACK #-} !Char,
  210                              alexStr :: {-# UNPACK #-} !ByteString.ByteString,
  211                              alexBytePos :: {-# UNPACK #-} !Int}
  212 
  213 alexInputPrevChar :: AlexInput -> Char
  214 alexInputPrevChar = alexChar
  215 
  216 alexGetByte (AlexInput {alexStr=cs,alexBytePos=n}) =
  217     case ByteString.uncons cs of
  218         Nothing -> Nothing
  219         Just (c, rest) ->
  220             Just (c, AlexInput {
  221                 alexChar = ByteString.w2c c,
  222                 alexStr =  rest,
  223                 alexBytePos = n+1})
  224 #endif

  226 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  227 -- Token positions
  228 
  229 -- `Posn' records the location of a token in the input text.  It has three
  230 -- fields: the address (number of characters preceding the token), line number
  231 -- and column of a token within the file. `start_pos' gives the position of the
  232 -- start of the file and `eof_pos' a standard encoding for the end of file.
  233 -- `move_pos' calculates the new position after traversing a given character,
  234 -- assuming the usual eight character tab stops.
  235 
  236 #if defined(ALEX_POSN) || defined(ALEX_MONAD) || defined(ALEX_POSN_BYTESTRING) || defined(ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING) || defined(ALEX_GSCAN) || defined (ALEX_POSN_STRICT_TEXT) || defined(ALEX_MONAD_STRICT_TEXT)
  237 data AlexPosn = AlexPn !Int !Int !Int
  238         deriving (Eq, Show, Ord)
  239 
  240 alexStartPos :: AlexPosn
  241 alexStartPos = AlexPn 0 1 1
  242 
  243 alexMove :: AlexPosn -> Char -> AlexPosn
  244 alexMove (AlexPn a l c) '\t' = AlexPn (a+1)  l     (c+alex_tab_size-((c-1) `mod` alex_tab_size))
  245 alexMove (AlexPn a l _) '\n' = AlexPn (a+1) (l+1)   1
  246 alexMove (AlexPn a l c) _    = AlexPn (a+1)  l     (c+1)
  247 #endif
  248 
  249 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  250 -- Monad (default and with ByteString input)
  251 
  252 #if defined(ALEX_MONAD) || defined(ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING) || defined(ALEX_MONAD_STRICT_TEXT)
  253 data AlexState = AlexState {
  254         alex_pos :: !AlexPosn,  -- position at current input location
  255 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD_STRICT_TEXT
  256         alex_inp :: Data.Text.Text,
  257         alex_chr :: !Char,
  258         alex_bytes :: [Byte],
  259 #endif /* ALEX_MONAD_STRICT_TEXT */
  260 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD
  261         alex_inp :: String,     -- the current input
  262         alex_chr :: !Char,      -- the character before the input
  263         alex_bytes :: [Byte],
  264 #endif /* ALEX_MONAD */
  265 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING
  266         alex_bpos:: !Int64,     -- bytes consumed so far
  267         alex_inp :: ByteString.ByteString,      -- the current input
  268         alex_chr :: !Char,      -- the character before the input
  269 #endif /* ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING */
  270         alex_scd :: !Int        -- the current startcode
  271 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD_USER_STATE
  272       , alex_ust :: AlexUserState -- AlexUserState will be defined in the user program
  273 #endif
  274     }
  275 
  276 -- Compile with -funbox-strict-fields for best results!
  277 
  278 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD
  279 runAlex :: String -> Alex a -> Either String a
  280 runAlex input__ (Alex f)
  281    = case f (AlexState {alex_bytes = [],
  282                         alex_pos = alexStartPos,
  283                         alex_inp = input__,
  284                         alex_chr = '\n',
  285 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD_USER_STATE
  286                         alex_ust = alexInitUserState,
  287 #endif
  288                         alex_scd = 0}) of Left msg -> Left msg
  289                                           Right ( _, a ) -> Right a
  290 #endif
  291 
  292 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING
  293 runAlex :: ByteString.ByteString -> Alex a -> Either String a
  294 runAlex input__ (Alex f)
  295    = case f (AlexState {alex_bpos = 0,
  296                         alex_pos = alexStartPos,
  297                         alex_inp = input__,
  298                         alex_chr = '\n',
  299 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD_USER_STATE
  300                         alex_ust = alexInitUserState,
  301 #endif
  302                         alex_scd = 0}) of Left msg -> Left msg
  303                                           Right ( _, a ) -> Right a
  304 #endif
  305 
  306 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD_STRICT_TEXT
  307 runAlex :: Data.Text.Text -> Alex a -> Either String a
  308 runAlex input__ (Alex f)
  309    = case f (AlexState {alex_bytes = [],
  310                         alex_pos = alexStartPos,
  311                         alex_inp = input__,
  312                         alex_chr = '\n',
  313 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD_USER_STATE
  314                         alex_ust = alexInitUserState,
  315 #endif
  316                         alex_scd = 0}) of Left msg -> Left msg
  317                                           Right ( _, a ) -> Right a
  318 #endif
  319 
  320 newtype Alex a = Alex { unAlex :: AlexState -> Either String (AlexState, a) }
  321 
  322 instance Functor Alex where
  323   fmap f a = Alex $ \s -> case unAlex a s of
  324                             Left msg -> Left msg
  325                             Right (s', a') -> Right (s', f a')
  326 
  327 instance Applicative Alex where
  328   pure a   = Alex $ \s -> Right (s, a)
  329   fa <*> a = Alex $ \s -> case unAlex fa s of
  330                             Left msg -> Left msg
  331                             Right (s', f) -> case unAlex a s' of
  332                                                Left msg -> Left msg
  333                                                Right (s'', b) -> Right (s'', f b)
  334 
  335 instance Monad Alex where
  336   m >>= k  = Alex $ \s -> case unAlex m s of
  337                                 Left msg -> Left msg
  338                                 Right (s',a) -> unAlex (k a) s'
  339   return = App.pure
  340 
  341 
  342 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD
  343 alexGetInput :: Alex AlexInput
  344 alexGetInput
  345  = Alex $ \s@AlexState{alex_pos=pos,alex_chr=c,alex_bytes=bs,alex_inp=inp__} ->
  346         Right (s, (pos,c,bs,inp__))
  347 #endif
  348 
  349 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING
  350 alexGetInput :: Alex AlexInput
  351 alexGetInput
  352  = Alex $ \s@AlexState{alex_pos=pos,alex_bpos=bpos,alex_chr=c,alex_inp=inp__} ->
  353         Right (s, (pos,c,inp__,bpos))
  354 #endif
  355 
  356 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD_STRICT_TEXT
  357 alexGetInput :: Alex AlexInput
  358 alexGetInput
  359  = Alex $ \s@AlexState{alex_pos=pos,alex_chr=c,alex_bytes=bs,alex_inp=inp__} ->
  360         Right (s, (pos,c,bs,inp__))
  361 #endif
  362 
  363 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD
  364 alexSetInput :: AlexInput -> Alex ()
  365 alexSetInput (pos,c,bs,inp__)
  366  = Alex $ \s -> case s{alex_pos=pos,alex_chr=c,alex_bytes=bs,alex_inp=inp__} of
  367                     state__@(AlexState{}) -> Right (state__, ())
  368 #endif
  369 
  370 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING
  371 alexSetInput :: AlexInput -> Alex ()
  372 alexSetInput (pos,c,inp__,bpos)
  373  = Alex $ \s -> case s{alex_pos=pos,
  374                        alex_bpos=bpos,
  375                        alex_chr=c,
  376                        alex_inp=inp__} of
  377                     state__@(AlexState{}) -> Right (state__, ())
  378 #endif
  379 
  380 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD_STRICT_TEXT
  381 alexSetInput :: AlexInput -> Alex ()
  382 alexSetInput (pos,c,bs,inp__)
  383  = Alex $ \s -> case s{alex_pos=pos,alex_chr=c,alex_bytes=bs,alex_inp=inp__} of
  384                     state__@(AlexState{}) -> Right (state__, ())
  385 #endif
  386 
  387 alexError :: String -> Alex a
  388 alexError message = Alex $ const $ Left message
  389 
  390 alexGetStartCode :: Alex Int
  391 alexGetStartCode = Alex $ \s@AlexState{alex_scd=sc} -> Right (s, sc)
  392 
  393 alexSetStartCode :: Int -> Alex ()
  394 alexSetStartCode sc = Alex $ \s -> Right (s{alex_scd=sc}, ())
  395 
  396 #if defined(ALEX_MONAD_USER_STATE)
  397 alexGetUserState :: Alex AlexUserState
  398 alexGetUserState = Alex $ \s@AlexState{alex_ust=ust} -> Right (s,ust)
  399 
  400 alexSetUserState :: AlexUserState -> Alex ()
  401 alexSetUserState ss = Alex $ \s -> Right (s{alex_ust=ss}, ())
  402 #endif /* defined(ALEX_MONAD_USER_STATE) */
  403 
  404 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD
  405 alexMonadScan = do
  406   inp__ <- alexGetInput
  407   sc <- alexGetStartCode
  408   case alexScan inp__ sc of
  409     AlexEOF -> alexEOF
  410     AlexError ((AlexPn _ line column),_,_,_) -> alexError $ "lexical error at line " ++ (show line) ++ ", column " ++ (show column)
  411     AlexSkip  inp__' _len -> do
  412         alexSetInput inp__'
  413         alexMonadScan
  414     AlexToken inp__' len action -> do
  415         alexSetInput inp__'
  416         action (ignorePendingBytes inp__) len
  417 #endif
  418 
  419 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING
  420 alexMonadScan = do
  421   inp__@(_,_,_,n) <- alexGetInput
  422   sc <- alexGetStartCode
  423   case alexScan inp__ sc of
  424     AlexEOF -> alexEOF
  425     AlexError ((AlexPn _ line column),_,_,_) -> alexError $ "lexical error at line " ++ (show line) ++ ", column " ++ (show column)
  426     AlexSkip  inp__' _len -> do
  427         alexSetInput inp__'
  428         alexMonadScan
  429     AlexToken inp__'@(_,_,_,n') _ action -> let len = n'-n in do
  430         alexSetInput inp__'
  431         action (ignorePendingBytes inp__) len
  432 #endif
  433 
  434 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD_STRICT_TEXT
  435 alexMonadScan = do
  436   inp__ <- alexGetInput
  437   sc <- alexGetStartCode
  438   case alexScan inp__ sc of
  439     AlexEOF -> alexEOF
  440     AlexError ((AlexPn _ line column),_,_,_) -> alexError $ "lexical error at line " ++ (show line) ++ ", column " ++ (show column)
  441     AlexSkip  inp__' _len -> do
  442         alexSetInput inp__'
  443         alexMonadScan
  444     AlexToken inp__' len action -> do
  445         alexSetInput inp__'
  446         action (ignorePendingBytes inp__) len
  447 #endif
  448 
  449 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  450 -- Useful token actions
  451 
  452 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD
  453 type AlexAction result = AlexInput -> Int -> Alex result
  454 #endif
  455 
  456 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING
  457 type AlexAction result = AlexInput -> Int64 -> Alex result
  458 #endif
  459 
  460 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD_STRICT_TEXT
  461 type AlexAction result = AlexInput -> Int -> Alex result
  462 #endif
  463 
  464 -- just ignore this token and scan another one
  465 -- skip :: AlexAction result
  466 skip _input _len = alexMonadScan
  467 
  468 -- ignore this token, but set the start code to a new value
  469 -- begin :: Int -> AlexAction result
  470 begin code _input _len = do alexSetStartCode code; alexMonadScan
  471 
  472 -- perform an action for this token, and set the start code to a new value
  473 andBegin :: AlexAction result -> Int -> AlexAction result
  474 (action `andBegin` code) input__ len = do
  475   alexSetStartCode code
  476   action input__ len
  477 
  478 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD
  479 token :: (AlexInput -> Int -> token) -> AlexAction token
  480 token t input__ len = return (t input__ len)
  481 #endif
  482 
  483 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING
  484 token :: (AlexInput -> Int64 -> token) -> AlexAction token
  485 token t input__ len = return (t input__ len)
  486 #endif
  487 
  488 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD_STRICT_TEXT
  489 token :: (AlexInput -> Int -> token) -> AlexAction token
  490 token t input__ len = return (t input__ len)
  491 #endif
  492 
  493 #endif /* defined(ALEX_MONAD) || defined(ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING) || defined(ALEX_MONAD_STRICT_TEXT) */
  494 
  495 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  496 -- Basic wrapper
  497 
  498 #ifdef ALEX_BASIC
  499 type AlexInput = (Char,[Byte],String)
  500 
  501 alexInputPrevChar :: AlexInput -> Char
  502 alexInputPrevChar (c,_,_) = c
  503 
  504 -- alexScanTokens :: String -> [token]
  505 alexScanTokens str = go ('\n',[],str)
  506   where go inp__@(_,_bs,s) =
  507           case alexScan inp__ 0 of
  508                 AlexEOF -> []
  509                 AlexError _ -> error "lexical error"
  510                 AlexSkip  inp__' _ln     -> go inp__'
  511                 AlexToken inp__' len act -> act (take len s) : go inp__'
  512 
  513 alexGetByte :: AlexInput -> Maybe (Byte,AlexInput)
  514 alexGetByte (c,(b:bs),s) = Just (b,(c,bs,s))
  515 alexGetByte (_,[],[])    = Nothing
  516 alexGetByte (_,[],(c:s)) = case utf8Encode' c of
  517                              (b, bs) -> Just (b, (c, bs, s))
  518 #endif
  519 
  520 
  521 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  522 -- Basic wrapper, ByteString version
  523 
  524 #ifdef ALEX_BASIC_BYTESTRING
  525 
  526 -- alexScanTokens :: ByteString.ByteString -> [token]
  527 alexScanTokens str = go (AlexInput '\n' str 0)
  528   where go inp__ =
  529           case alexScan inp__ 0 of
  530                 AlexEOF -> []
  531                 AlexError _ -> error "lexical error"
  532                 AlexSkip  inp__' _len  -> go inp__'
  533                 AlexToken inp__' _ act ->
  534                   let len = alexBytePos inp__' - alexBytePos inp__ in
  535                   act (ByteString.take len (alexStr inp__)) : go inp__'
  536 
  537 #endif
  538 
  539 #ifdef ALEX_STRICT_BYTESTRING
  540 
  541 -- alexScanTokens :: ByteString.ByteString -> [token]
  542 alexScanTokens str = go (AlexInput '\n' str 0)
  543   where go inp__ =
  544           case alexScan inp__ 0 of
  545                 AlexEOF -> []
  546                 AlexError _ -> error "lexical error"
  547                 AlexSkip  inp__' _len  -> go inp__'
  548                 AlexToken inp__' _ act ->
  549                   let len = alexBytePos inp__' - alexBytePos inp__ in
  550                   act (ByteString.take len (alexStr inp__)) : go inp__'
  551 
  552 #endif
  553 
  554 #ifdef ALEX_STRICT_TEXT
  555 -- alexScanTokens :: Data.Text.Text -> [token]
  556 alexScanTokens str = go ('\n',[],str)
  557   where go inp__@(_,_bs,s) =
  558           case alexScan inp__ 0 of
  559                 AlexEOF -> []
  560                 AlexError _ -> error "lexical error"
  561                 AlexSkip  inp__' _len  -> go inp__'
  562                 AlexToken inp__' len act -> act (Data.Text.take len s) : go inp__'
  563 #endif
  564 
  565 #ifdef ALEX_POSN_STRICT_TEXT
  566 -- alexScanTokens :: Data.Text.Text -> [token]
  567 alexScanTokens str = go (alexStartPos,'\n',[],str)
  568   where go inp__@(pos,_,_bs,s) =
  569           case alexScan inp__ 0 of
  570                 AlexEOF -> []
  571                 AlexError ((AlexPn _ line column),_,_,_) -> error $ "lexical error at line " ++ (show line) ++ ", column " ++ (show column)
  572                 AlexSkip  inp__' _len  -> go inp__'
  573                 AlexToken inp__' len act -> act pos (Data.Text.take len s) : go inp__'
  574 #endif
  575 
  576 
  577 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  578 -- Posn wrapper
  579 
  580 -- Adds text positions to the basic model.
  581 
  582 #ifdef ALEX_POSN
  583 --alexScanTokens :: String -> [token]
  584 alexScanTokens str0 = go (alexStartPos,'\n',[],str0)
  585   where go inp__@(pos,_,_,str) =
  586           case alexScan inp__ 0 of
  587                 AlexEOF -> []
  588                 AlexError ((AlexPn _ line column),_,_,_) -> error $ "lexical error at line " ++ (show line) ++ ", column " ++ (show column)
  589                 AlexSkip  inp__' _ln     -> go inp__'
  590                 AlexToken inp__' len act -> act pos (take len str) : go inp__'
  591 #endif
  592 
  593 
  594 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  595 -- Posn wrapper, ByteString version
  596 
  597 #ifdef ALEX_POSN_BYTESTRING
  598 --alexScanTokens :: ByteString.ByteString -> [token]
  599 alexScanTokens str0 = go (alexStartPos,'\n',str0,0)
  600   where go inp__@(pos,_,str,n) =
  601           case alexScan inp__ 0 of
  602                 AlexEOF -> []
  603                 AlexError ((AlexPn _ line column),_,_,_) -> error $ "lexical error at line " ++ (show line) ++ ", column " ++ (show column)
  604                 AlexSkip  inp__' _len       -> go inp__'
  605                 AlexToken inp__'@(_,_,_,n') _ act ->
  606                   act pos (ByteString.take (n'-n) str) : go inp__'
  607 #endif
  608 
  609 
  610 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  611 -- GScan wrapper
  612 
  613 -- For compatibility with previous versions of Alex, and because we can.
  614 
  615 #ifdef ALEX_GSCAN
  616 alexGScan stop__ state__ inp__ =
  617   alex_gscan stop__ alexStartPos '\n' [] inp__ (0,state__)
  618 
  619 alex_gscan stop__ p c bs inp__ (sc,state__) =
  620   case alexScan (p,c,bs,inp__) sc of
  621         AlexEOF     -> stop__ p c inp__ (sc,state__)
  622         AlexError _ -> stop__ p c inp__ (sc,state__)
  623         AlexSkip (p',c',bs',inp__') _len ->
  624           alex_gscan stop__ p' c' bs' inp__' (sc,state__)
  625         AlexToken (p',c',bs',inp__') len k ->
  626            k p c inp__ len (\scs -> alex_gscan stop__ p' c' bs' inp__' scs)                  (sc,state__)
  627 #endif
  628 alex_tab_size :: Int
  629 alex_tab_size = 8
  630 alex_base :: AlexAddr
  631 alex_base = AlexA#

  964 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  965 -- INTERNALS and main scanner engine
  966 
  967 #ifdef ALEX_GHC
  968 #  define ILIT(n) n#
  969 #  define IBOX(n) (I# (n))
  970 #  define FAST_INT Int#
  971 -- Do not remove this comment. Required to fix CPP parsing when using GCC and a clang-compiled alex.
  972 #  if __GLASGOW_HASKELL__ > 706
  973 #    define GTE(n,m) (GHC.Exts.tagToEnum# (n >=# m))
  974 #    define EQ(n,m) (GHC.Exts.tagToEnum# (n ==# m))
  975 #  else
  976 #    define GTE(n,m) (n >=# m)
  977 #    define EQ(n,m) (n ==# m)
  978 #  endif
  979 #  define PLUS(n,m) (n +# m)
  980 #  define MINUS(n,m) (n -# m)
  981 #  define TIMES(n,m) (n *# m)
  982 #  define NEGATE(n) (negateInt# (n))
  983 #  define IF_GHC(x) (x)
  984 #else
  985 #  define ILIT(n) (n)
  986 #  define IBOX(n) (n)
  987 #  define FAST_INT Int
  988 #  define GTE(n,m) (n >= m)
  989 #  define EQ(n,m) (n == m)
  990 #  define PLUS(n,m) (n + m)
  991 #  define MINUS(n,m) (n - m)
  992 #  define TIMES(n,m) (n * m)
  993 #  define NEGATE(n) (negate (n))
  994 #  define IF_GHC(x)
  995 #endif

  997 #ifdef ALEX_GHC
  998 data AlexAddr = AlexA# Addr#
  999 -- Do not remove this comment. Required to fix CPP parsing when using GCC and a clang-compiled alex.
 1000 
 1001 {-# INLINE alexIndexInt16OffAddr #-}
 1002 alexIndexInt16OffAddr :: AlexAddr -> Int# -> Int#
 1003 alexIndexInt16OffAddr (AlexA# arr) off =
 1004 #ifdef WORDS_BIGENDIAN
 1005   narrow16Int# i
 1006   where
 1007         i    = word2Int# ((high `uncheckedShiftL#` 8#) `or#` low)
 1008         high = int2Word# (ord# (indexCharOffAddr# arr (off' +# 1#)))
 1009         low  = int2Word# (ord# (indexCharOffAddr# arr off'))
 1010         off' = off *# 2#
 1011 #else
 1012 #if __GLASGOW_HASKELL__ >= 901
 1013   GHC.Exts.int16ToInt#
 1014 #endif
 1015     (indexInt16OffAddr# arr off)
 1016 #endif
 1017 #else
 1018 alexIndexInt16OffAddr = (Data.Array.!)
 1019 #endif
 1020 
 1021 #ifdef ALEX_GHC
 1022 {-# INLINE alexIndexInt32OffAddr #-}
 1023 alexIndexInt32OffAddr :: AlexAddr -> Int# -> Int#
 1024 alexIndexInt32OffAddr (AlexA# arr) off =
 1025 #ifdef WORDS_BIGENDIAN
 1026   narrow32Int# i
 1027   where
 1028    i    = word2Int# ((b3 `uncheckedShiftL#` 24#) `or#`
 1029                      (b2 `uncheckedShiftL#` 16#) `or#`
 1030                      (b1 `uncheckedShiftL#` 8#) `or#` b0)
 1031    b3   = int2Word# (ord# (indexCharOffAddr# arr (off' +# 3#)))
 1032    b2   = int2Word# (ord# (indexCharOffAddr# arr (off' +# 2#)))
 1033    b1   = int2Word# (ord# (indexCharOffAddr# arr (off' +# 1#)))
 1034    b0   = int2Word# (ord# (indexCharOffAddr# arr off'))
 1035    off' = off *# 4#
 1036 #else
 1037 #if __GLASGOW_HASKELL__ >= 901
 1038   GHC.Exts.int32ToInt#
 1039 #endif
 1040     (indexInt32OffAddr# arr off)
 1041 #endif
 1042 #else
 1043 alexIndexInt32OffAddr = (Data.Array.!)
 1044 #endif
 1045 
 1046 #ifdef ALEX_GHC
 1047 -- GHC >= 503, unsafeAt is available from Data.Array.Base.
 1048 quickIndex = unsafeAt
 1049 #else
 1050 quickIndex = (Data.Array.!)
 1051 #endif
 1052 
 1053 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1054 -- Main lexing routines
 1055 
 1056 data AlexReturn a
 1057   = AlexEOF
 1058   | AlexError  !AlexInput
 1059   | AlexSkip   !AlexInput !Int
 1060   | AlexToken  !AlexInput !Int a
 1061 
 1062 -- alexScan :: AlexInput -> StartCode -> AlexReturn a
 1063 alexScan input__ IBOX(sc)
 1064   = alexScanUser undefined input__ IBOX(sc)
 1065 
 1066 alexScanUser user__ input__ IBOX(sc)
 1067   = case alex_scan_tkn user__ input__ ILIT(0) input__ sc AlexNone of
 1068   (AlexNone, input__') ->
 1069     case alexGetByte input__ of
 1070       Nothing ->
 1071 #ifdef ALEX_DEBUG
 1072                                    Debug.Trace.trace ("End of input.") $
 1073 #endif
 1074                                    AlexEOF
 1075       Just _ ->
 1076 #ifdef ALEX_DEBUG
 1077                                    Debug.Trace.trace ("Error.") $
 1078 #endif
 1079                                    AlexError input__'
 1080 
 1081   (AlexLastSkip input__'' len, _) ->
 1082 #ifdef ALEX_DEBUG
 1083     Debug.Trace.trace ("Skipping.") $
 1084 #endif
 1085     AlexSkip input__'' len
 1086 
 1087   (AlexLastAcc k input__''' len, _) ->
 1088 #ifdef ALEX_DEBUG
 1089     Debug.Trace.trace ("Accept.") $
 1090 #endif
 1091     AlexToken input__''' len ((Data.Array.!) alex_actions k)
 1092 
 1093 
 1094 -- Push the input through the DFA, remembering the most recent accepting
 1095 -- state it encountered.
 1096 
 1097 alex_scan_tkn user__ orig_input len input__ s last_acc =
 1098   input__ `seq` -- strict in the input
 1099   let
 1100   new_acc = (check_accs (alex_accept `quickIndex` IBOX(s)))
 1101   in
 1102   new_acc `seq`
 1103   case alexGetByte input__ of
 1104      Nothing -> (new_acc, input__)
 1105      Just (c, new_input) ->
 1106 #ifdef ALEX_DEBUG
 1107       Debug.Trace.trace ("State: " ++ show IBOX(s) ++ ", char: " ++ show c ++ " " ++ (show . chr . fromIntegral) c) $
 1108 #endif
 1109       case fromIntegral c of { IBOX(ord_c) ->
 1110         let
 1111                 base   = alexIndexInt32OffAddr alex_base s
 1112                 offset = PLUS(base,ord_c)
 1113 
 1114                 new_s = if GTE(offset,ILIT(0))
 1115                           && let check  = alexIndexInt16OffAddr alex_check offset
 1116                              in  EQ(check,ord_c)
 1117                           then alexIndexInt16OffAddr alex_table offset
 1118                           else alexIndexInt16OffAddr alex_deflt s
 1119         in
 1120         case new_s of
 1121             ILIT(-1) -> (new_acc, input__)
 1122                 -- on an error, we want to keep the input *before* the
 1123                 -- character that failed, not after.
 1124             _ -> alex_scan_tkn user__ orig_input
 1125 #ifdef ALEX_LATIN1
 1126                    PLUS(len,ILIT(1))
 1127                    -- issue 119: in the latin1 encoding, *each* byte is one character
 1128 #else
 1129                    (if c < 0x80 || c >= 0xC0 then PLUS(len,ILIT(1)) else len)
 1130                    -- note that the length is increased ONLY if this is the 1st byte in a char encoding)
 1131 #endif
 1132                    new_input new_s new_acc
 1133       }
 1134   where
 1135         check_accs (AlexAccNone) = last_acc
 1136         check_accs (AlexAcc a  ) = AlexLastAcc a input__ IBOX(len)
 1137         check_accs (AlexAccSkip) = AlexLastSkip  input__ IBOX(len)
 1138 #ifndef ALEX_NOPRED
 1139         check_accs (AlexAccPred a predx rest)
 1140            | predx user__ orig_input IBOX(len) input__
 1141            = AlexLastAcc a input__ IBOX(len)
 1142            | otherwise
 1143            = check_accs rest
 1144         check_accs (AlexAccSkipPred predx rest)
 1145            | predx user__ orig_input IBOX(len) input__
 1146            = AlexLastSkip input__ IBOX(len)
 1147            | otherwise
 1148            = check_accs rest
 1149 #endif
 1150 
 1151 data AlexLastAcc
 1152   = AlexNone
 1153   | AlexLastAcc !Int !AlexInput !Int
 1154   | AlexLastSkip     !AlexInput !Int
 1155 
 1156 data AlexAcc user
 1157   = AlexAccNone
 1158   | AlexAcc Int
 1159   | AlexAccSkip
 1160 #ifndef ALEX_NOPRED
 1161   | AlexAccPred Int (AlexAccPred user) (AlexAcc user)
 1162   | AlexAccSkipPred (AlexAccPred user) (AlexAcc user)
 1163 
 1164 type AlexAccPred user = user -> AlexInput -> Int -> AlexInput -> Bool
 1165 
 1166 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1167 -- Predicates on a rule
 1168 
 1169 alexAndPred p1 p2 user__ in1 len in2
 1170   = p1 user__ in1 len in2 && p2 user__ in1 len in2
 1171 
 1172 --alexPrevCharIsPred :: Char -> AlexAccPred _
 1173 alexPrevCharIs c _ input__ _ _ = c == alexInputPrevChar input__
 1174 
 1175 alexPrevCharMatches f _ input__ _ _ = f (alexInputPrevChar input__)
 1176 
 1177 --alexPrevCharIsOneOfPred :: Array Char Bool -> AlexAccPred _
 1178 alexPrevCharIsOneOf arr _ input__ _ _ = arr Data.Array.! alexInputPrevChar input__
 1179 
 1180 --alexRightContext :: Int -> AlexAccPred _
 1181 alexRightContext IBOX(sc) user__ _ _ input__ =
 1182      case alex_scan_tkn user__ input__ ILIT(0) input__ sc AlexNone of
 1183           (AlexNone, _) -> False
 1184           _ -> True
 1185         -- TODO: there's no need to find the longest
 1186         -- match when checking the right context, just
 1187         -- the first match will do.
 1188 #endif
 1189 {-# LINE 90 "src/SAWScript/Lexer.x" #-}
 1190 cnst f p s   = f p s
 1191 via  c g p s = c p s (g s)
 1192 via' c g p s = c p (g s)
 1193 
 1194 scanTokens :: String -> [Token AlexPosn]
 1195 scanTokens str = go (alexStartPos, '\n', [], str)
 1196   where go inp@(pos, _, _, str) =
 1197             case alexScan inp 0 of
 1198               AlexEOF -> [TEOF pos "EOF"]
 1199               AlexError ((AlexPn _ line column),_,_,_) -> error $ "lexical error at " ++ (show line) ++ " line, " ++ (show column) ++ " column "
 1200               AlexSkip inp' len -> go inp'
 1201               AlexToken inp' len act -> act pos (take len str) :  go inp'
 1202 
 1203 lexSAW :: FilePath -> String -> [Token Pos]
 1204 lexSAW f = dropComments . map fixPos . scanTokens --alexScanTokens
 1205   where fixPos tok =
 1206           let (AlexPn _ sl sc) = tokPos tok
 1207               pos = case lines (tokStr tok) of
 1208                       [] -> Range f sl sc sl sc
 1209                       [l] -> Range f sl sc sl (sc + length l)
 1210                       (l:ls) -> Range f sl sc (sl + length ls) (length (last (l:ls)))
 1211           in tok { tokPos = pos }
 1212 
 1213 
 1214 readCode :: String -> String
 1215 readCode = reverse . drop 2 . reverse . drop 2
 1216 
 1217 readBin :: String -> Integer
 1218 readBin s = case readInt 2 isDigit cvt s' of
 1219               [(a, "")] -> a
 1220               _         -> error $ "Cannot read a binary number from: " ++ show s
 1221   where cvt c = ord c - ord '0'
 1222         isDigit = (`elem` "01")
 1223         s' | "0b" `isPrefixOf` s = drop 2 s
 1224            | "0B" `isPrefixOf` s = drop 2 s
 1225            | True                = s
 1226 
 1227 dropComments :: [Token Pos] -> [Token Pos]
 1228 dropComments = go 0
 1229   where go :: Int -> [Token Pos] -> [Token Pos]
 1230         go _  []                 = []
 1231         go !i (TCmntS _ _ : ts)  = go (i+1) ts
 1232         go !i (TCmntE _ _ : ts)
 1233          | i > 0                 = go (i-1) ts
 1234         go !i (t : ts)
 1235          | i /= 0                = go i ts
 1236          | True                  = t : go i ts
 1237 
 1238 
 1239 alexEOF = (TEOF (error "alexEOF") "")
 1240 
 1241 scan :: Monad m => FilePath -> String -> m [Token Pos]
 1242 scan f = return . lexSAW f
